# 035 Renames

## Rename Plan - 2026-04-09

## Recovered Provenance

- Recovered baseline snapshot: `6f058fd` with 89 original rows.
- Append snapshot: `7813d84` with the later 37-row `/src` expansion.
- The active table below keeps the recovered rows in deterministic order; provenance remains captured in the bullets above.
- Sorting order is now deterministic: first by `Crate`, then by full `Path`.

## Execution Authority Fence - 2026-04-13

- Direct execution scope is limited to the recovered rename table in this file plus
  the later `High-Confidence Delta` block.
- The raw 814-row matrix remains inventory-only evidence and must not be treated as
  an execution checklist.
- `Doublechecked No-Change Calls` remain protected non-goals until a later plan
  explicitly reopens them.
- Phase 035 rename execution remains file-first: file/path/include literals move
  before any symbol, signature, or callsite rename wave.

## Plan 17 Live Lane Split - 2026-04-13

| Rows | Scope | Live recheck | Lockstep literals | Phase 035 | Comments |

## Suffix-Lane Handoff - 2026-04-12

This section is the bounded handoff from `035-a2-suffixes.md` into the curated
rename lane.

Only declaration-backed `production-current` rows that the canonical suffix
source already approves for rename planning may enter this table. Raw suffix
inventory, filename-only rows, explicit exclusions, corrected rows, and live
compatibility lanes stay outside this suffix-lane handoff table.

| Suffix source row | Suggested rename target | Handoff class | Why this row is in scope | Paths | Phase 035 | Comments |
| --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |
| `default_v2` | `default` | active rename candidate | current fresh-backup KDF constructor while `legacy_v1` remains the explicit compatibility lane | `crates/z00z_wallets/src/core/backup/wallet_backup_kdf.rs`; `wallet_backup.rs`; `backup_exporter_impl.rs` | Ōøö’ĖÅ | Approved candidate only; no later Phase 035 summary proves the unsuffixed landing. |

### Suffix-Lane Keep Boundaries

- `==reserved-future==` suffix rows remain compatibility or retirement-review
  inputs only.
- Public V2 claim helper symbols such as `claim_stmt_hash_v2` stay outside this
  handoff until an explicit API-retirement decision says the public V2 surface
  can collapse safely.
- Single surviving `V1` rows remain symbol-review candidates, not mechanical
  rename work.
- Corrected inventory rows such as `CheckpointStmtV1` stay quarantined outside
  this suffix-lane handoff table.
- Public contract strings, filename-only rows, and corrected inventory rows do
  not enter this suffix-lane handoff table during Plan 05.
- Historical recovered tables and raw matrices elsewhere in this document may
  still record legacy sightings until their own cleanup passes reconcile them;
  that does not widen this suffix-lane handoff table.

## Doublecheck

- Provenance remains captured in the recovered snapshot bullets above; the active table now focuses on current rename decisions only.
- The sorted table preserves all 126 rows while making crate-local review deterministic.
- The earlier conservative scope remains intact: the recovered baseline and later append snapshot remain preserved in the provenance bullets above even though the active table no longer carries a dedicated provenance column.
- The suffix-lane handoff stays bounded to one declaration-backed active
  candidate and does not widen the suffix-lane handoff table to compatibility,
  filename, or public-contract rows.
- The active handoff candidate still points back to the canonical suffix source
  and remains planning-only evidence; it is not a direct instruction to rename
  source files without a later curated execution wave.

## ­¤öŹ Append 2026-04-10 - Long-Name / Bad-Name Audit

### Scope

- Requested crates: `crates/z00z_core`, `crates/z00z_crypto`, `crates/z00z_simulator`, `crates/z00z_storage`, `crates/z00z_utils`, `crates/z00z_wallets`
- Vendor exclusion respected: `crates/z00z_crypto/tari/`
- Scan narrowed to `fn` and `struct` declarations only for the long-name inventory pass

### Inventory Snapshot

- Over-5-word declaration hits: `814`
- Kind breakdown: `fn=808`, `struct=6`
- Crate breakdown:
  - `crates/z00z_core`: `65`
  - `crates/z00z_crypto`: `81`
  - `crates/z00z_simulator`: `133`
  - `crates/z00z_storage`: `96`
  - `crates/z00z_utils`: `41`
  - `crates/z00z_wallets`: `398`
- Observation: the raw inventory is dominated by descriptive test functions and stage/version tokens (`stage4`, `v2`, `z00z`) that inflate strict word splitting. The actionable table below is limited to high-confidence bad names and low-risk long-name fixes that remained sound after an independent doublecheck pass.

### Revalidated Existing Rows Already Recorded Above

- `mk_out_with_blind_for_tests` -> `test_make_output_with_blind`
- `OpenedWlt` -> `OpenedWallet`
- `WltSession` -> `WalletSession`
- `RedbWltStore` -> `RedbWalletStore`
- `with_wlt_session` -> `with_wallet_session`
- `default_wlt_store` -> `default_wallet_store`
- `with_output_dir_and_dependencies` -> `with_output_dir_and_time`
- `core_wallet_id_rpc_wallet` -> `parse_core_wallet_id`
- `persist_wlt_snapshot` -> `persist_wallet_snapshot`

### Doublechecked No-Change Calls

- `default_stage5_recipient_output_index`: keep as-is; the `output` segment matches the real config field and removing it weakens the contract.
- `derive_key_argon2id_32`: keep as-is; the `32` suffix carries a real output-size contract and aligns with the surrounding KDF API style.

## ­¤öŹ Append 2026-04-10 - Raw Matrix Of All 814 Over-5-Word Names

- Purpose: append-only full inventory of every current `>5`-word Rust symbol hit in the requested crate scope.
- Suggested-Name policy: this raw section now includes bulk candidate `Suggested-Name` values. Curated pros/cons-reviewed rename decisions remain the `High-Confidence Delta` block above.
- Candidate generation basis: reuse curated `Suggested-Name` values when the same symbol already appears above; otherwise apply one deterministic bulk heuristic: expand common shorthand, preserve the strongest verb/domain nouns, collapse numeric stage tokens, and target `<=5` words when the symbol shape allows it.
- No-op candidate rule: some rows keep the current spelling when the over-5 hit comes only from numeric or camel/digit word splitting and the existing identifier is already the most compact readable form.
- Scope: `crates/z00z_core`, `crates/z00z_crypto`, `crates/z00z_simulator`, `crates/z00z_storage`, `crates/z00z_utils`, `crates/z00z_wallets` (excluding Tari vendor code).
